      <div n="6" type="sthāna">
        <head>[Uttaratantra 31-66]</head>

        <div n="31" type="adhyāya">
          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 31: draft edition based on MS K]</head>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.1"><label>6.31.1</label> athāto revatīpratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.3"><label>6.31.3</label> aśvagandhājaśṛṅgī ca śārivātha purnarnnavā |
            <caesura/>
             sahavidārī ca tathā kaṣāyaḥ pariṣecane | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.4"><label>6.31.4</label> tailam abhyaṅgane kāyaṃ kuṣṭhe sarjarase tathā
            |
            <caesura/>
             palaṃ kaṣāyainalade tathā girikadaṃbake | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.5"><label>6.31.5</label> vaṭāś ca karṇṇakakubhadhātakītindūkeṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             kākolyādau gaṇecāpi pāṇīyaṃ sarpir iṣyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.6ab"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.6cd"><label>6.31.6cd</label> gṛdhrolūkapurīṣāṇi tathā yavaphalāghṛtaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.7"><label>6.31.7</label> saṃdhyayor ubhayoḥ kāryam etad uddhūpanaṃ śiśā
            |
            <caesura/>
             varuṇāriṣṭakamayaṃ rumakaṃ saindhavaṃ tathā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.8"><label>6.31.8</label> dhārayed yāpi satataṃ vacā putrakajīvake |
            <caesura/>
             śuklāḥ sumanaso lājapayaḥ śālyodanaṃ tathā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.9"><label>6.31.9</label> valin nivedya gotīrthe revatyaiprayatātmanā |
            <caesura/>
             saṃgame ca bhiṣak snānaṃ kuryād dhātrīkumārayoḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.10"><label>6.31.10</label> nānāvastradharādevī citramālyānulepanā |
            <caesura/>
             calatkuṇḍalinī śyāmā revatīte prasīdatu | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.11"><label>6.31.11</label> yām upāsannisatataṃ devyo vividhabhūṣaṇāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             lamvākarālāvinatā tathaiva vahuputrikā |
            <caesura/>
             raivatī śuṣkanāsā ca sā ca devī prasīdatām iti || </l>
          <p ana="trailer"> kumāra || 3 || ❈ || </p>
        </div>


        <div n="32" type="adhyāya">

          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 32: draft edition based on MS K]</head>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.1"><label>6.32.1</label> athātaḥ pūtanāpratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.3"><label>6.32.3</label> kapotavaṃkāharalaḥ varuṇaḥ pāribhadrakaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             āsphotā caiva yojyāḥ syur vālasya pariṣecane | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.4"><label>6.32.4</label> vacā vayaḥ sthā golomī haritālaṃ manaḥ śilā |
            <caesura/>
             kuṣṭhaṃ sarjarasaṃ caiva tailārthe vargam iṣyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.5"><label>6.32.5</label> hitaṃ ghṛtan tukākṣīryāḥ siddhaṃ madhurakeṣu
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             kuṣthatālīsakhadirāḥ rṣapajñane tathā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.6"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.7"><label>6.32.7</label> śaṇanākulakumbhīkā majjāno vadarasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             karkaṭāsthi ghṛtañ cāpi dhūpanaṃ saha sarṣapaiḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.8"><label>6.32.8</label> kākādanīñ citraphalāṃ vimvīṃ guñjāñ ca
            dhārayet |
            <caesura/>
             matsyodanañ ca kurvīta kṛśaram palalaṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             śarāvasampuṭakṛtam valiṃ śūnyagṛhe haret | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.9ab"><label>6.32.9ab</label> utsṛṣṭān nābhiṣekaś ca śiśoḥ snapanam
            iṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.9cd"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.10"><label>6.32.10</label> malināmvarasamvītā malinārūkṣamūrdhajā |
            <caesura/>
             śūnyāgāśrayādevī dārakaṃ pātu pūtanā iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.32.11"/>
          <p ana="trailer"> kumāra || 3 || ❈ || </p>

        </div>
        <div n="33" type="adhyāya">
          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 33: draft edition based on MS K]</head>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.1"><label>6.33.1</label> athātāndhapūtanāpratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.3"><label>6.33.3</label> tiktakadrumāṇāṃ patraiś ca kvāthaḥ kāryo
            vasecane |
            <caesura/>
             surā sauvīrakañ kuṣṭhaṃ haritālam manaḥ śilā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.4"><label>6.33.4</label> tathā sarjarasaṃ cāpi tailārtham apasaṃharet
            ||
            <caesura/>
             pippalīpippalīmūlaṃ vargam madhurakam madhuḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.5ab"><label>6.33.5ab</label> sālaparṇī vṛhatyau ca ghṛtārtham api
            vuddhimāṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.5cd"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.6"><label>6.33.6</label> purīśaṃ kaukkuṭaṃ keśāḥ ścarmma sarvppatvageṣu
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             jīrṇṇāñ ca bhikṣusaṃghāṭīṃ dhūpanāyopakalpayet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.7"><label>6.33.7</label> kukkuṭīṃ markaṭīvimvīm anantāś cāpi dhārayet
            ||
            <caesura/>
             māṃsamāmaṃ tathā pakvaśoṇitañ ca catuḥ pathe| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.8"><label>6.33.8</label> nivedyam antañ ca gṛhe śiśoḥ snapanam iṣyate
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.33.9"><label>6.33.9</label> karālapiṃgalā muṇḍā kaṣāyam varadhāriṇī |
            <caesura/>
             devī vālam imaṃ prītā rakṣatām andhapūtanā iti || </l>
          <p ana="trailer"> kumāra || || ❈ || </p>
        </div>


        <div n="34" type="adhyāya">
          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 34: draft edition based on MS K]</head>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.1"><label>6.34.1</label> athātaḥ śītapūtanāpratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.3"><label>6.34.3</label> viṃvīkāpitthaṃ sūrasaṃ tathā vilvapracīvalau |
            <caesura/>
             nandībhallātakañ cāpi pariṣeke vacārayet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.4"><label>6.34.4</label> vastamūtraṃ gavaṃ mūtramūstañ cāmaradārū ca |
            <caesura/>
             kuṣṭhañ ca sarvagandhañ ca tailārtham avacārayet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.5"><label>6.34.5</label> rohiṇīsarjakhadirapalāśakakubhatvacaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             niḥkvāthya tasminniḥ kvāthe sakṣīraṃ vipaceddhṛtaṃ| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.6"><label>6.34.6</label> gṛdhrolūkapurīṣāṇi vastagandhāṃ sahāṃ vacāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             nivasya patrāṇi tathā dhūpanārthaṃ prayojayet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.7"><label>6.34.7</label> dhārayed api guñjāñ ca lamvāṃ kākādanīn tathā
            |
            <caesura/>
             nadhyāṃ mudgadanaiś cāpi tarpayec chītapūtanāṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.8ab"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.8cd"><label>6.34.8cd</label> jalāyaśānte vālasya spanaṃñ copadiśyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.34.9"><label>6.34.9</label> mugdodanāśinī devī surāśoṇitapāyinī |
            <caesura/>
             jalāśayaratādevī pātu tvāṃ śītapūtanā iti || </l>
          <p ana="trailer"> kumāra || || 0 || </p>
        </div>
        <div n="35" type="adhyāya">
          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 35: draft edition based on MS K]</head>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.1"><label>6.35.1</label> athāto muṇḍikāpratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.3"><label>6.35.3</label> kapitthavilvau tarkārīvaṃśagandharvahastaka |
            <caesura/>
             kuverākṣī ca yojyāni vālasya pariṣecane | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.4"><label>6.35.4</label> svarasair bhṛṅgavṛkṣāṇāṃ tathaiva hayagandhayā
            | tailaṃ vasāṃ ca saṃyojya paced abhyañjanaṃ śiśāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.5"><label>6.35.5</label> madhūlikā payasyā ca tugākṣīdyo gaṇau na ca |
            <caesura/>
             madhuraiḥ pañcamūlyāś ca kanīyasyā ghṛtam pacet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.6"><label>6.35.6</label> yavāḥ sarjarasaḥ kuṣṭhaṃ sarpiścoddhūpanahitaṃ
            |
            <caesura/>
             dhārayed api jihvāś ca cāṣavaiḍālasatyajāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.7"><label>6.35.7</label> varṇakaṃ cūrṇakaṃ mālyamañjanām pārataṃ tathā
            |
            <caesura/>
             manaḥ śilāṃ copaharet goṣṭhamadhye valiṃ śuciḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.8ab"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.8cd"><label>6.35.8cd</label> mantrapūtābhir adbhiś ca tatraiva snapanam
            bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.35.9"><label>6.35.9</label> alaṃkṛtā rūpavatī subhagā kāmarūpiṇī |
            <caesura/>
             goṣṭhamadhyālayā devī pātu tvāṃ mukhamaṇḍikā iti || </l>
          <p ana="trailer"> kumāra || || 0 || </p>
        </div>
        <div n="36" type="adhyāya">
          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 36: draft edition based on MS K]</head>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.1"><label>6.36.1</label> athāto naigameṣapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.3"><label>6.36.3</label> vilvāgnimanthapūtīkāḥ kāśmaryāḥ pariṣecane |
            <caesura/>
             savījañ cāpi dhānyāmlam pariṣekapraśasyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.4"><label>6.36.4</label> priyaṅgu saralānantā śatapuṣpākuṭannaṭaiḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             pacet tailaṃ surātakradadhimastvāmlakāñjikaiḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.5"><label>6.36.5</label> pañcamūladvayakvāthaiḥ kṣīre madhurakeṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             paced ghṛtañ ca matimāṃ kharjūryā mastakena ca | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.6ab"><label>6.36.6ab</label> vacā vayasthā ¦ ¦ ¦ ¦ sahitāṃ jaṭilāṃ cāpi
            dhārayet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.6cd"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.7"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.8"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.9"><label>6.36.9</label> tilataṇḍulakaṃ mālyaṃ bhakṣāṃś ca vividhāni ca
            | kumārapitṛmeṣāya vṛkṣamūle nivedayet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.10ab"><label>6.36.10ab</label> adhastān kṣīravṛkṣasya snapanañ
            copadiśyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.10cd"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.36.11"><label>6.36.11</label> ajānanañ calākṣibhrū kāmarūpī mahāyaśāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vālaṃ vālapitā devo naigameṣo bhirakṣatām iti || </l>
          <p ana="trailer"> kumāra || || ❈ || </p>

        <div n="37" type="adhyāya">
          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 37: draft edition based on MS K]</head>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.1"><label>6.37.1</label> athāto grahotpattiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.2a"><label>6.37.2a</label> atha khalu van</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.3"><label>6.37.3</label> navaskandādayaḥ proktā bālānāṃ ya ime grahāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śrīmanto divyavapuṣo nārīpuruṣavigrahāṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.4"><label>6.37.4</label> ete guhasya ra kṛttikomāgniśūlibhiḥ | sṛṣṭāḥ
            śaravanasthāsya rakṣitasatmatejasā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.5"><label>6.37.5</label> strīvigrahāgrahā ye tu nānārūpā mayeritāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             devīnāṃ kṛttikānān te bhāgā rājasatāmatāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.6"><label>6.37.6</label> naigameṣas tu pārvatyāḥ sṛṣṭo meṣānano grahaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             kumāradhāro devasya guhasyātmodbhavasya vai | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.7"><label>6.37.7</label> skandāpasmāraṃ sañjayaḥ so 'gnināgnisamadyutiḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             saivaskandasakho nāmnā viśākha iti cocyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.8"><label>6.37.8</label> skandaḥ sṛṣṭo bhagavatā devena tripurāriṇā |
            <caesura/>
             bibharti cāparaṃ saṃjñaṃ kumāra iti saṃgrahaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.9"><label>6.37.9</label> bālalīlādharo yo 'yaṃ devo rudrāgnisambhavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mithyā bāleṣu bhavavāṃ na khalv eṣu pravarttate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.10"><label>6.37.10</label> kumāraskandasāmānyād atra kecid apaṇḍitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             gṛṇhātīty aparijñānād bruvate dehacintakāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.11"><label>6.37.11</label> tato bhagavati skande devasenāpatau kṛte |
            <caesura/>
             upatasthur grahās dyute dīptaśaktidharaṃ guhaṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.12"><label>6.37.12</label> ūcuḥ prāñjalaś caivanaṃ vṛttin no vidhdhātsv
            iti |
            <caesura/>
             teṣām arthe tataḥ skandaḥ śivaṃ devam acodayat | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.13"><label>6.37.13</label> tato grahāṃ tān uvāca bhagavāṃ bhaganetrahā
            |
            <caesura/>
             tairyagyonim mānuṣañ ca devañ ca tritayaṃ jagat | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.14"><label>6.37.14</label> parasparopakāreṇa varttate dhāryate tathā |
            <caesura/>
             devamanuṣyāṃ prīṇanti tairyagyonin tathaiva ca | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.15"><label>6.37.15</label> yathākālaṃ pravarttanta uṣṇaṃ
            varṣahimādribhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ijyābalinamaskārair japya homais tathaiva caḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.16"><label>6.37.16</label> samyak prayuktaiś ca naraiḥ prīṇayaṃty atu
            devatāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhāgadheyā vibhaktāś ca śeṣaṃ kiñcin na vidyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.17"><label>6.37.17</label> tad yuṣmākaṃ śubhā vṛttiḥ pūjāsv eva
            bhaviṣyati |
            <caesura/>
             kuleṣu yeṣu nejyaṃte devatāpitaras tathā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.18"><label>6.37.18</label> vrāhmaṇāḥ sādhavo vāpi guravo 'tithayas
            tathā
            <caesura/>
             nivṛtta śaucācāreṣu tathā klaśopajīviṣu | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.19"><label>6.37.19</label> utsannabhikṣavaliṣu tathā bhinnagṛheṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             gṛheṣu yeṣu te bālāms tān hiṃsaṃ dhvamaśaṅkitāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.20"><label>6.37.20</label> tatra vo vipulā vṛttiḥ pūjā caiva bhaviṣyati
            |
            <caesura/>
             evaṃ grahāḥ samutpannā bālā hiṃsanti cāpy ataḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.37.21"><label>6.37.21</label> grahopasṛṣṭā bālās tu duścikitsyatamāḥ
            smṛtāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vaikalyam maraṇam cāpi dhruvaṃ skandagrahe nṛṇām iti || </l>

        <div n="39" type="adhyāya">
          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 39: draft edition based on MS K]</head>


          <note>[This adhyāya is currently a rough version based on MSS NAK 5-333 and 699, being
            edited (2023-10-04).]</note>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.1"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.1</label> athāto jvarapratiṣedhaṃ adhyāyaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||<anchor n="SS.6.39.1-n1"/>
          </l>

          <ab corresp="#SS.6.39.1" type="apparatus">
            <list type="Note">
              <item corresp="#SS.6.39.1-n1">In reading <foreign>-utpatti</foreign>, the scribe of H
                may have been influenced by the title <foreign>grahotpatti</foreign> of the
                immediately preceding adhyāya in his manuscript (he omits the
                  <foreign>yonivyāpat</foreign> adhyāya).</item>
            </list>
          </ab>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.3.1"><label>6.39.3.1</label> atha khalu vatsasuśruta </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.3"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.3</label> yenāmṛtam apāṃ madhyād uddhṛtaṃ
            pūrvvajanmani |
            <caesura/>
             yato 'maratvaṃ saṃprāptās tridaśās tridiveśvarāḥ ||<anchor n="SS.6.39.3-n1"/>
          </l>

          <ab corresp="#SS.6.39.3" type="apparatus">
            <list type="Note">
              <item corresp="#SS.6.39.3-n1">Dalhaṇa (p. 671) reported Jejjaṭa's reading
                  <foreign>tridaśās tridaśeśvarāḥ</foreign>, which is a mixture of the readings of
                witnesses K and H.</item>
            </list>
          </ab>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.4"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.4</label> śiṣyās taṃ devam āsīnaṃ papracchuḥ
            suśrutādayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vraṇasyopadravāḥ proktā vraṇinām apy ataḥ paraṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.5"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.5</label> samāsato vyāsataś ca brūhi no
            bhiṣajām vara |
            <caesura/>
             upadraveṇa juṣṭasya vraṇaḥ kṛcchreṇa sidhyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.6"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.6</label> upadravāś ca vraṇinaḥ
            kṛcchrasādhytamo mataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             prakṣīṇabalamāṃsasya śeṣadhātuparikṣayāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.7ab"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.7ab</label> tasmād upadravān kṛtsnān vadasva
            vadatām vara || </l>
          
          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.7cd"/> 

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.8"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.8</label> teṣān tad vacanaṃ śrutvā prābravīd
            bhiṣajām varaḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             jvaram ādau pravakṣyāmi sa rogānīkarāṭ smṛtaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.9"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.9</label> rudrakopāgnisaṃbhūtaḥ
            sarvvabhūtapratāpanaḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             tais tair nnāmabhir anyeṣāṃ sattvānām parikīrttyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.10"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.10</label> janmādau nidhane caiva bhavatīha na
            saṃśayaḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             ataḥ sarvavikārāṇāṃ jvaro rājā prakīrttitaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.11"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.11</label> ṛte devamanuṣyebhyo nānyo viṣahate
            tu taṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.12"/>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.13"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.13</label> svedāvarodhaḥ santāpaḥ
            sarvvāṅgagrahaṇam tathā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.14"><label>1938 ed. 6.39.14</label> yugapad yatra roge tu jvara ity
            upadiśyate ||

          <ab corresp="#SS.6.39.19cd" type="apparatus">
            <list type="Emendation">
              <item corresp="#SS.6.39.19cd-n1">Witnesses N and H read <foreign>api-</foreign> for
                the emended reading <foreign>adhi-</foreign>. While both MSS seem to have read
                  <foreign>pa</foreign>, it should be noted that in the script of MS K,
                  <foreign>pa</foreign> and <foreign>dha</foreign> are somewhat similarly written.
                This suggests a reading <foreign>dha</foreign> that was misread early in the
                transmission.</item>

             sroto nirodhā virasaś ca vaktraṃ sītābhir adbhiś ca vivṛddhimeti |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.1"><label>6.57.1</label> athāto rocakapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.3"><label>6.57.3</label> doṣaiḥ pṛthak trividhasokasamucchrayāc ca
            bhaktāyaneṣu hṛdi cāvatate pragāḍhaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             nānne rucir bhavati taṃ bhiṣajo vikāraṃ bhaktopaghātam iha pañcavidhaṃ vadanti | | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.4"><label>6.57.4</label> hṛcchūlaśoṣavamathuḥ svarasaṃkṣayāc ca
            vātā<add/> sadāhamadatṛḍ vamane ca pittaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pittāt kaphena hṛdaye gurutāvilepaḥ śleṣmaprasekavamathuḥ śiraso rujañ ca | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.5"><label>6.57.5</label> sarvātmakaṃ trividhaliṃgam atho vadanti ||
            <caesura/>
             śokopaghātajam athānilalakṣaṇais tu |
            <caesura/>
             vātātmake virasam āsyam arocake tu pittena tiktakaṭukaṃ madhuraṃ kaphena | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.6"><label>6.57.6</label> sarvair upetam upadhārayasannipāte | dainyaṃ
            bhṛśam bhavati śokasamudbhave tu |
            <caesura/>
             vāṃtovacādir anile vidhivat pibec ca snehoṣṇatoyamadirānyatamena cūrṇṇaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.7"><label>6.57.7</label>
            kṛṣṇāviḍaṃgayavabhasmahareṇubhārgīrāsnailahiṃgulavaṇottamanāgarāṇāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pitte guḍāmbumadhurair vamanaṃ praśastaṃ lehaś ca saindhavasitāmadhusarpiriṣṭaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.8"><label>6.57.8</label> nimbāmbuccharditavataḥ kaphaje nupānaṃ
            rājadrumāmbu madhunā tu sadīpyakāḍhyaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇṇaṃ yad uktam atha vā tilaje tad eva sarvaiś ca sarvakṛtam evam upakrameta | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.9"><label>6.57.9</label>
            drākṣāpaṭolaviḍavetrakarīranimbamūrvābhayākṣabadarāgalakendravṛkṣāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bījaiḥ karañjanṛpavṛkṣabhavaiś ca piṣṭai lehaṃ pacet surabhimūtrayutaṃ yathāvat | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.10"><label>6.57.10</label> mustāvacākaṭukarohiṇinirdahanyas tulyātha
            vāpi rajanābhayasaṃprayuktā |
            <caesura/>
             mūtre vike dviradamūtrayutāḥ paced vā pāṭhāsamām ativiṣāṃ rajanāñ ca mukhyāṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.11"><label>6.57.11</label> maṇḍūkim arkam amṛtāṃ raśalāṃgalākhyāṃ mūtre
            paceta mahiṣasya vidhāṇavidvān |
            <caesura/>
             etān na santi caturo bhyasatas tu lehān gulmāruciś ca śikhisādahṛdāmayāś ca | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.12"><label>6.57.12</label> sātmyāsvadeśacaritāṃ vividhāṃś ca bhakṣyāṃ
            pānāni mūlaphalaṣāḍavarogayogāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             seved rasāṃś ca vividhāṃ vividhaiḥ prakārair bhuñjīta vāpi laghurūkṣamanaḥsukhāni | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.13"><label>6.57.13</label> āsthāpanaṃ vividham atra virecanañ ca kuryān
            mṛdūni śirasaś ca virecanāni |
            <caesura/>
             trīṇy ūṣaṇāni triphalāṃ rajanīdvayañ ca cūrṇṇīkṛtāni yavaśūkavimiśritāni | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.14"><label>6.57.14</label> kṣaudrāyutāni vitaren mukhadhāvanārthaṃm
            anyāni tiktakaṭukāni ca bheṣajāni |
            <caesura/>
             mustādirājaphalavargadaśāṃgasiddhaḥ kvāthair jayen madhuyutair vividhaiś ca lehaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.15"><label>6.57.15</label> mūtrāsavair guḍakṛtaiś ca tathāpy ariṣṭaiḥ
            kṣārāsavaiś ca madhumādhavatulyagandhaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             syād eṣa eva kaphavātaharo vidhiś ca | śātiṃ gate hutabhuji praśamāya tasya | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.16"><label>6.57.16</label> icchāvināśabhayajeṣu ca bādhakeṣu | bhāvād
            bhavāya vitaret khalu śalyatāpān |
            <caesura/>
             artheṣu cātipatiteṣu punarbhavāya paurāṇikaśrutimukhair avamānayeta iti || kāyaci || 20
            || 0 || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.17"><label>6.57.17</label> cchardi hikkā śvāsakāsaḥ svaraghātam
            athāparaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pratiśyāyaḥ krimiś caiva sodāvarttā visūcikā |
            <caesura/>
             arocakena ca tathā pūryate dvitīyo daśaḥ || ❈ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.1"><label>6.59.1</label> athāto mūtrāghātapratiṣedhaṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.2"><label>6.59.2</label> yadā mūtrayato jantoḥ mūtravego vihanyate |
            <caesura/>
             mūtrāghātaṃ vadanty etam aṣṭadhā sa tu vakṣyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.3"><label>6.59.3</label> vātena pittena kaphena sarvais tathābhighātaiḥ
            śakṛdaśmaribhyāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             tathāparaḥ śarkarayā sukaṣṭo mūtropaghātaḥ paṭhito ṣṭamas tu<del rend="crossed out"
              >ḥ</del> | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.4"><label>6.59.4</label> alpam alpaṃ bhṛśaṃpīḍya muṣkamehanabastibhiḥ
            <caesura/>
             saṃtudyamānaḥ kṛcchreṇa vātāghātena mehate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.5"><label>6.59.5</label> pītam vāpy atha vā raktaṃ muṣkamehanabastibhir
            <caesura/>
             agnineva ca dahṛmbhiḥ pittāghātena mehate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.6"><label>6.59.6</label> samunnaddhodaraḥ kṛcchrān muṣkamehanabastibhiḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             saṃhṛṣṭaromā gurubhiḥ śleṣmāghātena mehate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.7"><label>6.59.7</label> dāhaśītarujāviṣṭo nānāvarṇṇam muhur muhus
            <caesura/>
             tāmyamānaḥ sa kṛcchreṇa sannipātena mehate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.8"><label>6.59.8</label> mūtravāhiṣu śalyena kṣateṣv abhihateṣu vā |
            <caesura/>
             srotaḥsu mūtrāghātas tu jāyate bhṛṣadāruṇaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.9"><label>6.59.9</label> vātāghātena liṅgāni tasya tulyāni nirddiśet ||
            <caesura/>
             śakṛtas tu pratīghātād vāyur viguṇatāṃ gataḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.10"><label>6.59.10</label> sādhmānañ ca samūlañ ca mūtrasaṅgaṃ karoti
            ca ||
            <caesura/>
             aśmarīsambhavasyoktaṃ mūtraghātasya lakṣaṇaṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.11"><label>6.59.11</label> aśmarī śarkarā caiva śṛṇu kīrttayato mamaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śarkarāyā viśeṣan tu śṛṇu kīrttayato mama | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.12"><label>6.59.12</label> pacyamānaṃ tu pittena śoṣyamānan tu vāyunā |
            <caesura/>
             śleṣmaṇā veṣṭitaṃ cūrṇṇaṃ śarkarety abhisañjñitaṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13"><label>6.59.13</label> hṛtpīḍā vepathuḥ śūlaḥ kukṣāv agniś ca
            durbalaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tābhir bhavati mūrcchā ca mūtrāghātaś ca dāruṇaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13i"><label>6.59.13i</label> ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi
            mūtrāghātacikitsitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             kāryaṃ bhaved yathā yac ca śṛṇu kīrttayato mama ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13ii"><label>6.59.13ii</label> kaṣāyāny tha kalkāś ca lehāḥ svedās
            tathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             hitā syur mūtraghāteṣu tathaivottarabastayaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13iii"><label>6.59.13iii</label> ervvārubījakalkaḥ syāc
            chlakṣṇapiṣṭaukṣasammitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dhānyāmlbapeyo lavaṇo mūtrāghātena pīḍitaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13iv"><label>6.59.13iv</label> surāṃ sauvarcalavatīm pradhānāṃ prapiben
            naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             jīrṇṇabhuktaḥ sadā bhuñjaṃ saguḍaṃ śāntim arcchati |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13v"><label>6.59.13v</label> madhūdakena saṃloḍya karṣaṃ kuṃkumakasya
            vā |
            <caesura/>
             rātrau paryuṣitam pūtaṃ piben mūtrarujāpahaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13vi"><label>6.59.13vi</label> dāḍimāṃmblayutaṃ madyaṃ
            śuṇṭhījīrakasaṃyutaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pītvā surāṃ salavaṇāṃ mūtrakṛcchrāt pramucyate |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13vii"><label>6.59.13vii</label> pṛthakparṇyādivargañ ca svadaṃṣṭrāñ
            caiva tatsamaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             ardhaprasthena dugdhasya paced ardhāḍhakodake |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13viii"><label>6.59.13viii</label> kṣīrāvaśiṣṭam āhṛtya pūtaṃ sarpir
            vidhūpitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             śītīkṛtaṃ pibed enaṃ mūtrakṛcchraharan naraḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13ix"><label>6.59.13ix</label> gardasya śakṛd vāpi vājināṃ vā gavāṃ
            tathā |
            <caesura/>
             rasasya tasya kuḍavaṃ piben mūtrarujāpahaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13x"><label>6.59.13x</label> haridrāṃ madhukaṃ mūrvāṃ mustakaṃ devadāru
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             pibed akṣasamāṃ kalkāṃ payasā mūtrapīḍitaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xi"><label>6.59.13xi</label> triphalāṃ śūkṣmapiṣṭaṃ vā kalkaṃ
            badarasammitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             vāriṇā lavaṇīkṛtya piben mūtrarujāpahaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xii"><label>6.59.13xii</label> drākṣārasasya kuḍavaṃ piben
            mūtrarujāharaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             nidigdhikāyāḥ svarasaṃ pūtaṃ kuḍavasammitaṃ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xiii"><label>6.59.13xiii</label> mūtradoṣaharam pītvā naraḥ
            sampadyate sukhī ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xiv"><label>6.59.13xiv</label> prapīḍyāmalakānām vā rasaṃ
            kuḍavasammitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pītvāgadībhavej jantur mūtradoṣeṇa pīḍitaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xv"><label>6.59.13xv</label> mūtradoṣe pibed vāpi hiṃgvelāpānasaṃyutā
            |
            <caesura/>
             pānālābhe hitam vāpi svetataṇḍudhāvanaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xvi"><label>6.59.13xvi</label> elāhiṃguyutaṃ kṣīraṃ sarpirmiśram
            piben naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūtradoṣo viśudhyarthaṃ śukradoṣaharañ ca tat |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xvii"><label>6.59.13xvii</label> palāśakṣāram āhṛtya
            saptakṛtvāpariśrutaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pāyayet tailasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ mūtradoṣeṇa pīḍitaṃ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xviii"><label>6.59.13xviii</label> adhyardhaprasṛtaṃ vāpi tathā sa
            labhate sukhaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pāṭalīkṣāram āhṛtya palāśakṣāravac ca taṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xix"><label>6.59.13xix</label> vilvasiṃhīyavanāḍaṃ palāśaḥ
            pāribhadrakaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             eṣāṃ kṣāram parisrāvya surayā saha saṃsṛjet ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xx"><label>6.59.13xx</label> tatra kalkān imāṃ dadyād
            badarāsthisamanvitāṃ ||
            <caesura/>
             varāṃgamūṣakāṇy elā ślakṣṇaṃ dṛśadi pīṣayet |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xxi"><label>6.59.13xxi</label> ekatraitat samāloḍya pibec charkarayā
            saha |
            <caesura/>
             eteṣv eva pacet sarpis taṃ lihen madhunā saha |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.13xxii"><label>6.59.13xxii</label> saguḍakṣārasaṃyuktaṃ mūtrakṛcchrāt
            pramucyate ||
            <caesura/>
             etat sarvaṃ prayoktavyaṃ mūtrāghāte vijānatā ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.14"><label>6.59.14</label> mūtradoṣeṣu kṛcchreṣu tena sampadyate gadaḥ
            |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.15"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.16"><label>6.59.16</label> aśmarīśarkarāhetoḥ pūrvam uktaṃ cikitsitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             prasamīkṣya yathānyāyaṃ bhiṣak tān api yojayet |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.17"><label>6.59.17</label> śvadaṃṣṭrāditaṭekuñci hapuṣāṃ kaṇṭakārikāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             kālāṃ śatāvarīṃ rāsnāṃ varuṇaṃ sirivālikāṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.18"><label>6.59.18</label> vidārigandhādi saṃhṛtya tābhiḥ sa tṛvṛtāṃ
            pibet ||
            <caesura/>
             tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā tat peyaṃ tena vāpy anuvāsanaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.19"><label>6.59.19</label> dadyād uttarabastiñ ca vātakṛcchropaśāntaye
            ||
            <caesura/>
             svadaṃṣṭrāsvarase tailaṃ saguḍakṣīranāgaraṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.20"><label>6.59.20</label> paktvā samyak pibet tac ca dadyād
            anilaruggharaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             utpalaṃ tṛṇakākolīnyagrodhādīgaṇe kṛtaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.21"><label>6.59.21</label> pītaṃ ghṛtaṃ pittakṛcchraṃ nāśayet kṣīram
            eva vā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.22"><label>6.59.22</label> ebhir eva kṛtaṃ snehaṃ trividheṣv eva

            <caesura/>
             hitaṃ virecanaṃ cekṣukṣīradrākṣārasair yutaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.23"><label>6.59.23</label> rasaṃ mauṣakamustādi varuṇādau ca saṃbhṛtaṃ
            |
            <caesura/>
             tailaṃ tathā yavāgvādi kaphāghāte praśasyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.24"><label>6.59.24</label> yathādoṣocchrayaṃ kuryād etām eva ca sarvaje
            |
            <caesura/>
             phalguvṛścikadarbhāśmasāracūrṇṇaṃ ca vāriṇā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.25"><label>6.59.25</label> surekṣurasadarbhāmbupītaṃ kṛcchrarujāpahaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             tathābhighātaje kuryāt sadyo vraṇacikitsitaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.26"><label>6.59.26</label> mūtrakṛcchre sadā cāsya kāryā vā vātikī
            kriyā ||
            <caesura/>
             svedāvagāhāvabhyaṃgaḥ basticūrṇṇakriyās tathā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.27"><label>6.59.27</label> sakṛjje vā tathānyau tu muddhiṣṭau
            kriyāvidhīti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.60.2"><label>6.60.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ śruṇu vatsa
            suśruta || <anchor n="SS.6.60.2-n1"/>
          </l>

          <ab corresp="#SS.6.60.2" type="apparatus">
            <list type="Notes">
              <item corresp="#SS.6.60.2-n1"> One of the only two places in the Nepalese version
                where this phrase appears. The other is Suśrutasaṃhitā 5.1.2. At that location, a
                scribe of witness H added the marginal phrase <foreign>atha khalu
                  vatsasuśrutaḥ</foreign>.</item>
            </list>
          </ab>

            <caesura/>
             doṣāṇyaṃ tatra matimāṃ triṣaṣṭīnāṃ prayojayet | </l>

            <caesura/>
             pañcānukramate yogān amvlaś catura eva ca | </l>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.7"><label>6.63.7</label> trīṇyaitā gacchati raso lavaṇaḥ kaṭuko dvayaṃ
            |
            <caesura/>
             tiktaḥ kaṣāyamanveti te dvikā daśa pañca ca || </l>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.8"><label>6.63.8</label> tadyathā | madhurāmvlau | madhuralavaṇau |
            madhurakaṭukau | madhuratiktau | madhurakaṣāyau | ete pañcānukrāntā madhureṇa ||
            amvlalavaṇaḥ | amvlakaṭukaḥ | amvlatiktaḥ | amvlakaṣāyaḥ | te catvāro nukrāntā amvlena |
            lavaṇakaṭuḥ | lavaṇatiktaḥ | lavaṇakaṣāyaḥ | ete nukrāntās trayo lavaṇaina || kaṭutiktaḥ
            | kaṭukaṣāyaḥ | dvāv anukrāntau kaṭukena || tiktakaṣāyaḥ | eka evānukrāntas tiktaina ||
            ete pañcadaśa dvikasaṃyogāḥ vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.9"><label>6.63.9</label> trikāna ta ūdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | ādau
            prayujyamānas tu madhuro daśa gacchati |
            <caesura/>
             ṣaḍamvlo lavaṇas tasmād adham ekaṃ rasaḥ kaṭuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.10"><label>6.63.10</label> madhurāmvlakaṭuḥ | madhurāmvlatiktaḥ |
            madhurāmvlalavaṇakaṭuḥ | madhurāmvlalavaṇatiktaḥ | madhurāmvlalavaṇakaṣāyaḥ |
            madhurakaṭutiktaḥ | madhurakaṭutiktaḥ | madhurakaṭukaṣāyaḥ || madhuratiktakaṣāyaḥ | evam
            eteṣān daśānāṃ trikaśaṃyogānāṃ mādau madhuraḥ prayujyate || amvlalavaṇakaṭuḥ |
            amvlalavaṇatiktaḥ | amvlalavaṇakaṣāyaḥ | amvlakaṭutiktaḥ | amvlakaṭukaṣāyaḥ |
            amvlatiktakaṣāyaḥ |evam eṣāṃ ṣaṇṇyamādāv amvlaḥ prayujyate || lavaṇakaṭutiktaḥ |
            lavaṇakaṭukaṣāyaḥ | lavaṇatiktakaṣāyaḥ | evam eteṣāṃ trayāṇāmādau lavaṇaḥ prayujyate ||
            kaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ | evam eṣa eka evādau kaṭukaḥ | evam ete trikasaṃyogā viṃśatir
            vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.11"><label>6.63.11</label> catuṣkānata ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             catuṣkarasasaṃyoge madhuro daśa gacchati |
            <caesura/>
             amvlacaturo yāti lavaṇastveka eva tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.12"><label>6.63.12</label> madhurāmvlalavaṇakaṭukaḥ |
            madhurāmlalavaṇatiktaḥ | madhurāmvlalavaṇakaṣāyaḥ | madhurāmvlakaṭutiktaḥ |
            madhurāmvlakaṭukaṣāyaḥ | madhurāmvlatiktakaṣāyaḥ | madhuralavaṇakaṭutiktaḥ |
            madhuralavaṇakaṭukaṣāyaḥ | madhuralavaṇatiktakaṣāyaḥ | madhuralavaṇatiktakaṣāyaḥ |
            madhurakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ | evam eṣāṃ daśānāṃ catuṣkasaṃyogānāmādau madhuraḥ prayujyate ||
            amvlalavaṇakaṭutiktaḥ | amvlalavaṇakaṭukaṣāyaḥ | amvlalavaṇatiktakaṣāyaḥ |
            amvlakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ | m eṣāṃ cartuṇṇāmādāvamvlaḥ | lavaṇakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ | evam eṣa
            eka evādau lavaṇaḥ | evam ete pañcadaśa catuṣkasaṃyogāḥ | pañcadaśa vyākhyātāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.13"><label>6.63.13</label> pañcakānata ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             pañcakāṃ pañca madhuraḥ ṣaṭkamamvlas tu gacchati | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.14"><label>6.63.14</label> madhurāmvlalavaṇakaṭutiktaḥ |
            madhurāmvlalavaṇakaṭukaṣāyaḥ | madhurāmvlalavaṇatiktakaṣāyaḥ |
            madhurāmlakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ | madhuralavaṇakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ | evam eṣāṃ
            madhurāmvlakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ || madhuralavaṅakaṭutiktakaṣāya iti || evam eṣāṃ pañcānāṃ
            pañcakasaṃyogānāmādau madhuraḥ prayujyate || amvlalavaṇakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ | evam
            ekasyādāv amvlaḥ | evam ete ṣaṭ pañcakāḥ vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.15"><label>6.63.15</label> ṣaṭkam ekam ata ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ ||
            madhurāmvlalavaṇakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ | ekas tu evam ekaḥ ṣaṭkasaṃyogāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.16"><label>6.63.16</label> ekaikaśaś ca ṣad rasā bhavanti | prākāśyena
            | madhuraḥ | amvlaḥ | lavaṇaḥ | kaṭukaḥ | tiktaḥ | kaṣāyaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.63.17"><label>6.63.17</label> evam ete triṣaṣṭirasayogāḥ vyākhyātāḥ |

             doṣabhedāt | dviṣaṣṭyās te prayoktavyā vicakṣaṇair iti || </l>

        <div n="65" type="adhyāya">

          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 65: draft edition based on MS K]</head>

          <head>[Adhyāya 65]</head>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.1"><label>1938 ed. 6.65.1</label> athātas tantrayuktyuddeśaṃ
            nāmādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.3"><label>1938 ed. 6.65.3</label> tatra dvātriṃśat tantrayuktayo
            bhavanti |
            <caesura/>
             tad yathā | adhikaraṇam | yogaḥ | padārthaḥ | hetvarthaḥ | uddeśaḥ | nirdeśaḥ |
            upadeśaḥ | apadeśaḥ | pradeśaḥ | atideśaḥ | apavargaḥ | vākyaśeṣaḥ | arthāpattiḥ |
            viparyayaḥ | prasaṅgaḥ | ekāntaḥ | anekāntaḥ | pūrvapakṣaḥ | nirṇṇayaḥ | anumatam |
            vidhānam | anāgatāpekṣaṇam | atikrāntāpekṣaṇaṃ | saṃśayaḥ | vyākhyānam | svasaṃjñā |
            nirvacanam | nidarśanam | niyogaḥ | vikalpaḥ | samuccayaḥ | ūhyam iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.4"><label>1938 ed. 6.65.4</label> atrāha | āsāṃ yuktīnāṃ kiṃ prayojanam
            | ucyate | vākyayojanam arthayojanañ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.5"><label>1938 ed. 6.65.5</label> ślokau cātra bhavataḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             asadvādiprayuktānāṃ<anchor n="SS.6.65.5-n1"/> śabdānāṃ pratiṣedhanam |
            <caesura/>
             svavākyasiddhir api ca kriyate tantrayuktibhiḥ || </l>

          <ab corresp="#SS.6.65.5" type="apparatus">
            <list type="Note">
              <item corresp="#SS.6.65.5-n1">We have adopted the vulgate reading here, although it is
                highly unlikely to be original. In MS H, this pāda appears to read <foreign
                  xml:lang="sa">asadaprayuktānāñ ca</foreign>. This is unmetrical, the compound is
                unusual, and there is an unexplained <foreign xml:lang="sa">ca</foreign>. There have
                been interventions in MS K by a second hand, and also there is a hole in the
                manuscript just at this point. The ante correctionem reading of K is unclear but
                appears to be closer to the reading of H than to the vulgate reading. These factors
                make it hard to reconstruct what a plausible and correct older reading might have
                been. For the impact on the meaning of this text, see notes to the
                translation.</item>
            </list>
          </ab>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.6"><label>1938 ed. 6.65.6</label> vyatyāsoktās tu ye hy arthā līnā ye
            cāpy anirmalāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             leśoktā ye ca kecit syus teṣāñ cāpi prasādhanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.7"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.8"><label>1938 ed. 6.65.8</label> tatra yam artham adhikṛtyocyate tad
            adhikaraṇam | yathā rasaṃ doṣaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.9"><label>1938 ed. 6.65.9</label> yena vākyaṃ yujyate sa yogaḥ | yathā
            vyatyāsenoktānāṃ sannikṛṣṭaviprakṛṣṭānāṃ padārthānām ekīkaraṇam ||<anchor
              n="#SS.6.65.9-n1"/>
            <caesura/>
             tailaṃ pibec cāmṛtavalli<pc> </pc><app>
              <lem>nimba</lem>
              <rdg wit="#JKT">vilva</rdg>
            </app><pc> </pc><app>
              <lem>haṃsāhvayā</lem>
              <rdg wit="#JKT">hiṃsrābhayā</rdg>
            </app><pc> </pc>vṛkṣakapippalībhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             siddhaṃ balābhyāñ ca sadevadāru hitāya nityaṃ galagaṇḍaroge ||<anchor n="SS.6.65.9-n2"/>
            <caesura/>
             siddhaṃ pibed iti prathamaṃ vaktavye <app>
              <lem>dvitīye pāde</lem>
              <rdg wit="#JKT">tṛtīyapāde</rdg>
            </app>
            <app>
              <lem>siddhaṃ</lem>
              <rdg wit="#JKT">siddham iti</rdg>
            </app> prayuktam |
            <caesura/>
             evan dūrasthānām api padārthānām ekīkaraṇaṃ yogaḥ || </l>

          <ab corresp="#SS.6.65.9" type="apparatus">
            <list type="Note">
              <item corresp="#SS.6.65.9-n1">The sentence, <foreign>yathā... ekīkaraṇam </foreign>,
                does not appear in the vulgate but an almost identical reading appears in Ḍalhana's
                commentary on this section.</item>
            </list>
            <list type="Testimonia">

              <item corresp="#SS.6.65.9-n2">
                <ref
                  target="https://saktumiva.org/wiki/wujastyk/susrutasamhita/04-su.ci-1-20/provisional-edition_cikitsasthana_01-20?upama_scroll=SS.4.18.47"
                    ><foreign>Suśrutasaṃhitā 4.18.47</foreign></ref>. For this section in the
                  <foreign>Cikitsāsthāna</foreign> there is only one witness viz., H, in the
                Nepalese version. It has a minor variant reading in the second line. Instead of
                  <foreign>siddhaṃ balābhyāṃ ca sadevadāru</foreign>, it reads <foreign>siddhaṃ
                  balābhyāṃ sahadevadāru</foreign>. The variant reading in the vulgate as
                  <foreign>°hiṃsrābhayā°</foreign> instead of <foreign>haṃsāhvayā</foreign> is not
                found in the actual occurrence of the verse in the <foreign>Cikitsāsthāna</foreign>,
                where it is identical with its reading of the <foreign>tantrayukti</foreign> section
                in the Nepalese version. The following quote from Vṛnda's <title>Siddhayoga</title>
                also supports the reading of the Nepalese recension and the reading in the
                  <foreign>Citkitsāsthāna</foreign> of the vulgate. <emph>Siddhayoga</emph>
                <ref
                  target="https://archive.org/details/VrndaMadhava1894/page/n171/mode/1up?view=theater"
                  >41.10</ref>: <foreign>tailaṃ pibec cāmṛtavallinimbahaṃsāhvayāvṛkṣakapippalībhiḥ |
                  siddhaṃ balābhyāṃ ca sadevadāru hitāya nityaṃ galagaṇḍaroge ||</foreign>
              </item>
            </list>
          </ab>

        <div n="66" type="adhyāya">

          <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 66: draft edition based on MS K]</head>

          <head>[Adhyāya 66]</head>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.1"> athāto doṣabhedavikalpam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.3"> aṣṭāṅgāyurvedavidaṃ kāśirājam mahīpatiṃ |<cb/>
            <caesura/>
             cchinnaśāstrārthasandehaṃ sūkṣmāgādhamivodadhiṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.4"> viśvāmitrasutaḥ śrīmāṃ suśrutaḥ paripṛcchati ||
            <caesura/>
             dviṣaṣṭirdoṣabhedā ye purastātparikīrttitāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.5"> kati tatraikaśo jñeyā viṃśo vāpy athavā triśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tasya<cb/> tad vacanaṃ śrutvā saṃśayacchinmahātapāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.6"> prītātmā nṛpaśārdūla suśrutāyāha tattvataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             trayo doṣā dhātavaś ca pūrīśaṃ mūtram eva ca | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.7"> dehaṃ sandhārayanty ete hy avyāpannā rasair hitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             puruṣaḥ ṣoḍaṣakalaḥ prāṇāś caikādaśaiva ye | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.8ab"> rogāṇāñ ca sahasraṃ yac chata viṃśatir eva ca | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.8cd"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.9"> vyāsataḥ kīrttitan tadvibhinnā doṣāsu yo guṇāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dviṣaṣṭidhā bhavanty ete bhūyiṣṭham iti niścayaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.10"> traya eva pṛthag doṣāḥ dviśo nava samādhikāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             trayodaśādhikaikadvihīnamadhyordhvalakṣaṇaiḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.11"> tribhir pañcāśad etan tu sahaivaṃ kṣayam āgataiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             hīnamadhyādhikādvekakṣīṇavṛddhās tathāpare </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.12"> dvādaśaiva samākhyātā rogayonir dviṣaṣṭidhā |
            <caesura/>
             miśrā dhātumalairaiva yānty asaṃkhyeyatām api | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.13"> tasmāt prasaṃgaṃ saṃyamya doṣabhedavikalpanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rogaṃ viditvopacared rasabhedair yathe ritaiḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.14"> bhiṣak karttātha karaṇaṃ rasā doṣāś ca kāraṇaṃ ||
            <caesura/>
             kāryam ārogyam evaikam anārogyam athāpi vā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.14a"> taśmāt sādhu viditvetāṃ rasadoṣavikalpaṇāṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.14b"> bhiṣajabheṣajaṃ kāryaṃ prāṇyaṃ hanyan yathā kṛtāṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.15"> adhyāyānāñ ca tuḥ ṣaṣṭyā grathitārthapadakramaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             etad eva viśeṣeṇa tantram uttaram ṛddhimat | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.16"> spagūḍhārthagambhīram agādhaṃ mandacetasāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             yathākramaṃ yathāpraśnaṃ yathā tatvaṃ yathā vidhiṃ | </l>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.16a">yathā pratijñañ ca mayā bhavatāṃ parikīrttitaṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.17" met="upajāti"> sahottaran tv etad adhītya tantraṃ svāyaṃbhuvaṃ taṃ
              vidhi<pc> </pc>kīrttitena |
            <caesura/>
             na hīyate rthāṃ manaso bhyupetād evaṃ vaco brāhmyam atīva satyam iti || ❈ ||</l>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.17i">mūtradoṣo mūtrāghāto yonyamānūṣa eva ca ||
            <caesura/>
             apasmāronmādakañ caiva rasabhedas tathaiva ca |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.17ii"> svastharakṣāvidhāṇañ ca tantrayuktiś ca doṣabhit |
            <caesura/>
             ity ebhir darśakaṃ proktaṃ punaḥ kāyacikitsite || ❈ ||</l>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.colophon1">samāptañ cedaṃ sahottaratantram ity ato nighaṇṭur bhaviṣyati
            || ❈ || </l>


        </div>

        <div type="colophon">

          <head>[<foreign xml:lang="en">Colophon</foreign>]</head>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.colophon2" met="Sragdharā"> rājye śrīmānadeve pṛthusitayaśasi
            prodyadinduprakāśe
            <caesura/>
             kāle puṇyārjjanasya sakalajanamanohlādiramye vasante
            <caesura/>
             varṣe caikottare 'smiṃs tritayaśatagate mādhave māsi śukle
            <caesura/>
             saptamyāṃ puṣya ṛkṣe daśaśatakiraṇe vāsare siddhayoge </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.colophon3" met="Sragdharā">
            utpattyādyambuvelākulavividharujagrāhajuṣṭātiraudre
            <caesura/>
             saṃsāre sāgare 'smiñ jagad idam akhilaṃ glāninam sampravīkṣya
            <caesura/>
             tasmāc chrīharṣacandro niratiśayaghṛṇābhāvito moktukāmaḥ
            <caesura/>
             prītyā caigaṃ <sic>prākhilat</sic> suśrutākhyam </l>

          <ab corresp="#SS.6.66.colophon3" type="apparatus">
            <list type="Notes">
              <item>It is hard to understand how a word ending in <foreign>-gaṃ</foreign>, or any
                accusative, could precede <foreign>prākhilat</foreign> or even <foreign>pra
                  akhilan</foreign>. Some readers have emended <foreign xml:lang="sa"
                  >prākhilat</foreign> to <foreign xml:lang="sa">prālikhat</foreign>, a rare verb,
                but one that at least governs the accusative. We do not see metathesis elsewhere in
                this scribe's work, which is generally very accurate, so we consider the emendation
                unlikely. With so many words missing from this passage, we consider that emendation
                is not useful.</item>

              <item>We read <foreign>-harṣacandro</foreign> which could be the name of the scribe.
                But the following <foreign>nnirati-</foreign> is hard to construe. If we read the
                ablative <foreign>-harṣacandrān</foreign>, it solve the problem of
                  <foreign>-nn-</foreign> but is also hard to construe.</item>
            </list>
          </ab>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.66.colophon4"> śrīgaṇadevadevakuladūnī gvalakanivāsino vaidyavasuvarmaṇaḥ
            pustakam idaṃ paṭhitvārtham avagamya sarvasattvānām upadeśaṃ vidhātuṃ pratipāditam |
            atas tad ādhikrayābhyāṃ tad gotrajena kenacin na kañcid dātavyam | yadā nopakriyate
            tadāsmān eva pratyarpaṇīyam iti || </l>


        </div>

      </div>
    </body>
  </text>
